413 
414 inline cFont *NEW_CFONTCALIBRI40()
415 {
416  cImage *img = new cImage();
417  cLoadPNG(img, CFONTCALIBRI40_BYTEARRAY, sizeof(CFONTCALIBRI40_BYTEARRAY));
418 
419  cFont *font = new cFont();
420  font->m_charset.m_base = CFONTCALIBRI40_CHARSET_BASE;
421  font->m_charset.m_lineHeight = CFONTCALIBRI40_CHARSET_LINEHEIGHT;
422  font->m_charset.m_width = CFONTCALIBRI40_WIDTH;
423  font->m_charset.m_height = CFONTCALIBRI40_HEIGHT;
424  font->m_charset.m_pages = CFONTCALIBRI40_CHARSET_PAGES;
425  for (int i=0; i<256; i++)
426  {
427  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_x = CFONTCALIBRI40_CHARSET[8*i ];
428  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_y = CFONTCALIBRI40_CHARSET[8*i+1];
429  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_width = CFONTCALIBRI40_CHARSET[8*i+2];
430  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_height = CFONTCALIBRI40_CHARSET[8*i+3];
431  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_xOffset = CFONTCALIBRI40_CHARSET[8*i+4];
432  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_yOffset = CFONTCALIBRI40_CHARSET[8*i+5];
433  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_xAdvance = CFONTCALIBRI40_CHARSET[8*i+6];
434  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_page = CFONTCALIBRI40_CHARSET[8*i+7];
435  }
436  font->m_charset.preProcess();
437 
438  font->m_texture->setImage(std::shared_ptr<cImage>(img));
439 
440  return (font);
441 }
